Important News

Another Instigating Trick by the Japanese 72

▲Yazaki and Others Attempt to Entice Northeast Military Officers

North China Correspondence: The Advanced Military Studies Research Class of the Northeast Military Academy was established in February of the 17th year of the Republic of China and the first class of students, totaling about 50 people, graduated in March of the 19th year and were assigned to various brigades for apprenticeships. In January of this year, the second class of students also graduated and were assigned to various brigades, following the example of the first class. Some of them have already taken positions such as staff officers. When the class was opened, in order to pre-store staff talents, it was necessary to have the enlightenment and guidance of those proficient in the strategy and tactics of the army, navy, and air force. Three Japanese instructors, Urasumi E, Suda Tadashi, and Yazaki Kanju, were hired to take on the role. Therefore, the Japanese instructors have a teacher-student relationship with the general students. However, since the Shenyang Incident, the instructors have all entered the Kwantung Army Headquarters to take up positions. Because the students of the class are scattered in various brigades of the Northeast Army, they even thought of instigating the students to betray the army, revolt and return to Shenyang, and cooperate with the Japanese army, stationed in the area around Dahu Mountain. Zhang Tingchu, the staff officers of the Liu and Gao regiments, were students in the class. Yesterday, they received two letters of incitement from Suda Tadashi and Yazaki Kanju. The content of the letters was absurd and unreasonable. The regiment reported it to the Border Defense Commander's Office for investigation and prohibition. The original text of the letters is extracted below to show that the Japanese are doing everything they can to instigate and divide our three eastern provinces.

▲Letter 1: Greetings. We have now driven out the warlords and political bandits with accumulated crimes in the three eastern provinces. The rest are all good people, so we want to build a peaceful world for these good people. If you can discern the current situation, abandon those great evils and warlords, and join the good people in building an ideal and peaceful kingdom, you will be practicing the true way of loving the country and protecting the people, which is what protectors of the country should do, and can be believed to be the only way forward. If you only aggravate the crimes of the warlords, what difference is there between you and a national traitor? We do not want you to support the crimes of the warlords and act as their accomplices, but wish that you would plan for your future happiness. Therefore, we dare to offer you our advice. If you believe it, return to your hometown as soon as possible and work hard with your fellow villagers to build a new world of paradise. We are extremely anxious and look forward to it. We wish you all the best. From Suda Tadashi and Yazaki Kanju, instructors of the Advanced Military Studies Research Class, respectfully to Staff Officer Liu Ziton and Staff Officer Gao Fanwu.

▲Letter 2: Greetings. It is deeply regrettable that an incident has unfortunately broken out between China and Japan this time. However, the Japanese people, for the sake of 70 million people, are striving for the peaceful development of Manchuria and Mongolia, which we believe you fully understand. Cooperation with your country in the peaceful development of the Chinese nation is the most important thing for the peace of East Asia and the happiness of the people of China and Japan. However, the sovereigns of the warlords of your country and some people around them have prevented Japan's legitimate hopes and have planned and organized anti-Japanese and insulting activities, using inhumane means to prevent the peaceful development of Japan's 70 million people and lead them to death. They even dared to carry out violent acts to destroy the South Manchuria Railway, which led the Japanese military to punish the military power holders in order to ensure the lifeblood of the South Manchuria Railway. Now, the old warlords and old regimes of the three northeastern provinces have all been destroyed. The rest are good people. Now, we are implementing good policies in the four northeastern provinces and building a truly peaceful ideal country, wanting to live a life of mutual happiness and welfare, which is worthy of confidence. Therefore, there are now newly formed troops. You have received advanced military education, have a thorough understanding of the world situation, and are all talented people who can seize the opportunity. Therefore, we hope that you will return to your hometown as soon as possible and build a peaceful environment, and leave the old warlords who are about to collapse, and strive for the formation of this new army and the construction of peace. If you return, it will not only be your happiness, but also the happiness of world peace. We are anxiously waiting to hear from you. We wish you all the best and hope that you will convey this meaning to your classmates and take action quickly. Yazaki Kanju, instructor of the Advanced Military Studies Research Class, 26 Inaba-cho, Fengtian Japanese Station.

Japanese Military Monitors Xi Qia 73

▲Exhausting All Efforts But Failing to Please

▲Anyone with a Conscience Should Know to Repent

Harbin Correspondence: Since the establishment of the puppet government of Jilin, finances have been extremely strained. The reserves in the provincial treasury had already been robbed clean by the Japanese. The operating expenses of various agencies must be scraped together with great effort from the districts under the control of Soehito and the Japanese military. Still, a large amount of military pay must be provided to the Japanese military every month. If they are slightly dissatisfied, the Japanese will summon them for reprimands. Xi Qia is quite embarrassed by this, so he requested Japanese Commander Honjo to use the protection of the Japanese army to send personnel to take over the tax collection agencies in important towns such as Changchun and Harbin. If there are any difficulties, the Japanese military will provide armed support. The Japanese agreed. Therefore, Xi Qia appointed Sun Qichang to manage the Yalu River Lumber Company and manage logging in the Yalu River area. He appointed Wei Zonglian as the Director of the Jilin-Heilongjiang Salt Transport Bureau, took over the Changchun Salt Transport Tax Bureau, and imprisoned the former director. The above-mentioned agencies are all the main sources of revenue for the Northeast. Xi Qia sacrificed his life to seize them for the Japanese. Yesterday, Xi issued an order to the various agencies, the text of which is recorded below: "In accordance with the fact that the Provincial Governor's Office of this province has been temporarily organized and established, all organizational outlines and the date of my appointment as Governor have been circulated in the past. This time, the incident occurred suddenly. I was acting as the head of both military and civil affairs, and I did not dare to act rashly and mislead the area, nor did I want to delay and sit idly by, watching the disaster. Since I had received the order of non-resistance, I immediately convened emergency meetings with military, political, and local groups, deciding that the troops in the provincial capital would be moved to the suburbs to avoid conflict, so that the merchants and residents were fortunate enough to be safe when the Japanese troops entered the city. Later, compelled by the situation, I temporarily organized the Governor's Office in order to unite the province and await future resolution. I feel that my virtue is thin and I dare to take on difficult tasks. However, the local people are attached to me with great righteousness, and temporarily no one is responsible, so I had to take on the task reluctantly. The circumstances are not of my own volition, and I hope that you will all understand. The leaders of various agencies, the county magistrates of various counties, and the directors of various tax bureaus have all worked together for many years. At this time of upheaval, they should prioritize the local people, be respectful of their duties, and work together to overcome difficulties. This is what I hope." After this order was issued, Ren Dafeng, the head of the Jilin Provincial Tax Bureau, obeyed Xi's order and sent Jin Yaoting (formerly an investigator at the Harbin Stamp Tax Office) to Harbin to take over the Binjiang Stamp Tax Office. A few days before, the Binjiang Stamp Tax Office had received an order from the Jilin Governor's Office, instructing it to remit the tax revenue to the provincial capital. The office did not respond. On the 26th, Jin Yaoting, the newly appointed officer, and his assistant Zhang Qian, sent Han Yuming and Xia Zhihan to see Li Changyin, the duty officer at the Stamp Tax Office, holding two official documents from Jilin, urging Li to expedite the handover. Li replied that the office was an agency under the Jilin Provincial Government and only knew how to follow the orders of the old provincial government. Chairman Zhang Jiang issued a telegram strictly forbidding compliance with the orders of the Jilin puppet government. He could not disobey Chairman Zhang's telegram and betray the puppet provincial government. He stated that Mr. Jin, the so-called new duty officer, had not received an order from Chairman Zhang to come here, and that he had no need to discuss anything with him. Seeing that Li's attitude was very resolute, Han and the others fled with the official documents. Because Jin Yaoting was Li's subordinate, after Han left, Li immediately sent someone to look for Jin. However, Jin, seeing that the situation was unfavorable, took a car and fled to Jilin. After investigating the situation, it was found that he had embezzled more than 200 Harbin silver dollars. The office is handling the matter in accordance with the usual procedures for public officials who embezzle funds and flee. On the one hand, they are reporting the circumstances of Jilin's sending personnel to take over the Stamp Tax Office to the Deputy Commander's Headquarters in Beiping, and on the other hand, they are issuing a telegram to inform all agencies and legal entities in the city of the true nature of Jilin's sending personnel to take over the Binjiang Stamp Tax Office this time. Furthermore, Xi Qia is now aware that the League of Nations has decided to order Japan to withdraw its troops, and Jilin's small empire has been confirmed to be a dream. He is deeply afraid that if the Japanese army withdraws, his personal position will not be guaranteed, and even his life may be in danger. Therefore, he secretly sent someone to Beiping to explain to Zhang Zuoxiang that his taking office and reorganizing the provincial government were all due to Japanese coercion, and that he had no such ambition. The matter was heard by the Japanese, who expressed great dissatisfaction. In addition to severely scolding Xi Qia, they also cancelled Xi's South Mansion and set up a large number of police officers at Xi's residence for surveillance. Xi's every move is being closely monitored. Anyone entering to meet with Xi must be inspected by the Japanese military. Official documents and even Xi's personal private letters must also be inspected. At this time, Xi Qia is truly in a situation where he cannot please anyone. (October 31st)

The So-Called Pending Issues of the Japanese Are Like This (Continued) 74

39. Forcibly Laying the Railway Through the Sakakibara Farm. In the 14th year of the Taisho era (1925), China obtained Sakakibara's promise regarding commercial leases and began laying the railway across the Beiling Farm, across the Choujingning Line, and to Huangtun, connecting to the Aviation Institute. At that time, the Fengtian Consulate General requested a method for paying rent for the use of the land. China claimed that the commercial lease contract was invalid. On June 27th of the 4th year of the Showa era (1929), Sakakibara was forced to remove the railway tracks by force. The farm had been formally recognized by the Chinese authorities for a commercial lease contract in the name of Sakakibara's younger brother, Uramoto Seizaburo, on May 6th of the 8th year of the Taisho era (1919).

40. Oppressing Japanese Residents in Fengtian City. Fengtian was opened to foreign residence and trade based on the 1903 Sino-American Commercial Treaty. Chinese officials in Fengtian set up a commercial port area outside Fengtian City and used this as a limit, forbidding foreigners from residing and doing business. They stubbornly insisted on their improper claim, ignoring repeated protests from Japan and related countries. They used methods of persecution against Japanese residents in the city to force them to leave. As a result, only 44 households remain in the city recently.

41. Oppressing Japanese Residents in Sanxing City. Sanxing City in Jilin Province was opened based on the Manchuria Treaty Accessory Book in the 28th year of the Meiji era (1895). Chinese officials made the same improper claim as in Fengtian and directly and indirectly oppressed Japanese residents in Sanxing City, making it difficult for them to live and do business. Currently, only five or six households remain. It is absolutely impossible for new residents and businesses to enter.

42. Oppressing Japanese Telephones in Fengtian City. Based on the Sino-Japanese Telegraph Agreement of the 41st year of the Meiji era (1908), Japan has reserved the right to operate telephones between the South Manchuria Railway Attached Land in Fengtian and Fengtian City. Two years ago, Chinese officials came to discuss the revision of urban areas in Fengtian Province and requested the relocation of telephone poles, changing the wires to lead-covered wires and reducing the number of telephone poles. Construction in the city was completed at the end of last year. By August of this year, the Fengtian Telecommunications Administration used some minor technical excuses to obstruct the connection work in the commercial port area, greatly hindering Japanese operations.

43. The Statute for Punishing Traitors to the Nation. (A) In the 4th year of the Taisho era (1915), the Fengtian Provincial Government, disregarding the treaties of Manchuria and Inner Mongolia, enacted a provisional statute for punishing traitors to the nation in July of the 4th year of the Showa era (1929) with the aim of harming the commercial lease rights of Japanese people engaged in commerce, industry, and agriculture in South Manchuria. They secretly ordered local officials to strictly prohibit foreigners from mortgaging or leasing land. Those who violated the statute would be sentenced to death or life imprisonment and fines.

Page 9

Excerpts from Important News 75

Gold, June of the 6th year of the Showa Era. After several revisions, the right regulations were changed to "Punishment Rules for Illegal Sale of National Land", trampling on the most important rights of Japanese people under the treaty. As a result of the promulgation of the right regulations, the aforementioned treaty became a dead letter. Not only is it impossible to obtain commercial lease rights in the future, but also the vested rights before the promulgation of this rule are gradually being taken back. For example, in March of the 4th year of the Showa Era, the Dongya Industrial Company of Mentai Village, Panyang County, leased 24 mu of land from a Chinese person, Li Yunfei, for 10,000 yuan. The Liaoning Provincial Government, by a decision of the committee, sentenced the right landlord to death under threat. In January of the 5th year of the Showa Era, the Dongya Industrial Company rescued the life of the landlord in question by acquiring the land title related to the case. This is a fact. As a result of the promulgation of the right illegal decree, in the past one or two years: 1. The county magistrate of Xinmin County sold land in Qigongtai in the county to Japanese people and imprisoned the landlords. 2. In Liuhe County, because a Chinese person, Zhao Shuhuan, leased land to Dongya Industrial Company, his land was confiscated and the Japanese manager was expelled (Dongshan Farm issue). 3. In Benxi County, a landlord was imprisoned and attempts were made to confiscate the coal mine on the grounds that a Chinese person leased a coal mountain to a Japanese person. 4. In Ji'an County, a Chinese person rented a house to a Japanese police station, and the head of the household was imprisoned. 5. Liaoning Province, regarding the scattered rice paddy management by Koreans in various places, followed the usual practice of dismissing existing lease agreements and cultivation contracts, and adopted a policy of converting them into simple employment contracts. Examples are too numerous to mention. (B) Jilin Province, like Fengtian Province, issued a "Prohibition Order on the Illegal Sale of National Land", disregarding the land ownership of Koreans based on the Gando Convention. Moreover, in various places in Jilin Province, Koreans are not only unable to buy land, but their cultivation contract terms are also subject to interference.

44. Obstructing Korean Residence and Farming: Recently, Chinese authorities in various parts of Manchuria have directly and indirectly suppressed the residence and farming of Koreans. In addition to the aforementioned obstruction of land lease cultivation contracts, new regulations have been issued to expel immigrants, prohibit renting of houses, hinder business operations, and force Chinese landlords and heads of households to not only order Koreans to vacate, but also use force in some cases. For example, 1. In June of this year, Jilin provincial authorities attempted to expel Koreans in Wanbaoshan and improperly interfered with the cultivation contracts between landlords and Koreans. 2. In July of the same year, Jilin Province, under the pretext of suppressing communists in Taolaizhao, expelled many innocent Korean farmers who had recently immigrated there. 3. Around August of the same year, in Tongliao, Chinese authorities exploited a civil dispute over the so-called misdiagnosis issue between a Korean doctor and a patient's family, forcibly prohibiting the doctor's business and forcibly evicting him. All such instances are too numerous to mention.

45. Illegal Arrests and Punishments of Koreans: Recently, Chinese authorities in the three northeastern provinces have disregarded treaties and arbitrarily arrested and imprisoned Koreans in Manchuria, mostly without any judicial procedures, sentencing them to imprisonment for several months or even more than a year. There are still more than 60 people in this category in the Fengtian Prison, about 40 in Dunhua, more than 130 in Jilin, and about 40 in Harbin.

46. Denying the Japanese Extraterritoriality Judgments of the Jilin Provincial Court: According to the judgment text of the Jilin Provincial Court on a secret accusation against a certain Korean, it is recognized that he has Japanese nationality. However, since the trade treaty with Japan has expired and is invalid, Japanese people do not have extraterritorial rights and must abide by the judgments of Chinese courts.

47. Failure to Comply with the Gando Convention: The Gando Convention stipulates that Koreans have the right to own land. However, China secretly issued a secret order prohibiting the illegal sale of national land, prohibiting Koreans from obtaining land ownership. In addition, Koreans have the freedom to export rice, but China secretly prevents this. The Koreans in Gando are greatly hit economically because they are not allowed to sell rice to the Korean peninsula across the border (the price of rice in Gando is about half the price of that in Korea). Furthermore, the Gando Convention stipulates that the Japanese consul must be notified regarding the lives of Koreans when they are defendants, but this is not implemented (see the previous item on the Ji-Hui line).

48. The Spread of Anti-Japanese Teaching Materials: In recent years, the Chinese government has incorporated many anti-Japanese materials into textbooks for national general education, cultivating a vengeful sentiment towards Japan among young citizens, which violates international faith and is a major event that goes against the fundamental meaning of Sino-Japanese friendship.

49. Anti-Japanese Propaganda by the Northeast Culture Society: The society is an organ of the Fengtian authorities and often broadcasts anti-Japanese content. The most notable example is the natural fire in the Dashan coal mine in Fushun in February of this year (called an explosion, but not to that extent), where no one died, but it was propagated that pit workers had died in the explosion. Japan protested but it was not cancelled.

50. Anti-Japanese Movement by the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association: The Liaoning National Diplomacy Association was organized in June of the 4th year of the Showa Era with anti-Japanese activities as its main purpose. Recently, it has been publishing its official magazine, holding daily gatherings, and using newspapers to vigorously spread malicious propaganda against Japan, leading to extreme deterioration of Sino-Japanese relations.

51. Oppression of the "Shengjing Times": The "Shengjing Times", a Chinese-character newspaper operated by Japanese in Fengtian, is the most authoritative media outlet in Manchuria, enjoying high credibility at home and abroad. However, in cases where its fair editorials are unfavorable to the Fengtian authorities, official power is abused to oppress it. There are many such instances. A recent notable example is the thorough obstruction of its distribution for about ten months from the 2nd to the 3rd year of the Showa Era, preventing delivery and making its business virtually impossible, causing enormous damage. Oppression continued thereafter, as was the case from June to August last year. Furthermore, from July to August of this year, the director of the Fengtian Public Security Bureau secretly colluded with the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association to arrest and imprison the newspaper's powerful vendors in Fengtian at the Public Security Bureau, subjecting them to indirect and despicable persecution.

52. Discriminatory Treatment in Issuing Domestic Travel Permits: Around October of last year, the Fengtian and Liaoyuan negotiators, aiming to prohibit Japanese people from traveling to areas west of Taonan and areas north of Jilin Province, and recently also in Huludao, which is competing with Dalian, restrictions were placed on Japanese travel. Compared with those of other foreigners, Japanese passports are subject to discriminatory treatment with restrictive endorsements. Japan has repeatedly protested, but not only has there been no reflection, but recently instructions have also been issued to negotiators in Tieling, Liaoyang, Andong, Yingkou, Tonghua, Hailong, etc., to impose restrictions similar to those in Fengtian and Liaoyuan.

53. Obstructing the Tongliao Farm: Regarding the farm operated by Dongya Industrial Company in Tongliao, when constructing flood control dikes this spring, the county Public Security Bureau, accompanied by a large number of police officers, set fire to the coolie huts and drove away the coolies working there.

54. The Nakamura Captain Incident: Captain Nakamura led Isugi Entaro and a Mongolian and a Russian on a trip to the Xing'an reclamation area. On July 26th of this year, they were ambushed and captured by the 3rd Regiment of the Soviet-Outer Mongolian Border Government stationed troops and all were killed. The facts are extremely clear. The Japanese side has repeatedly engaged in strong negotiations, but the Fengtian authorities initially denied the facts. When denial became impossible, they used various excuses to try to evade responsibility. (End)

▲ Telegram Urging Peace Talks: To Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Nanjing, Mr. Wang Jingwei, Mr. Hu Hanmin, Mr. Sun Ke, Mr. Cai Yuanpei, and Mr. Li Shizeng in Shanghai, The national crisis is increasingly urgent, the actions of the Japanese army are expanding, and the credibility of the League of Nations is precarious. The moment of survival or demise will be decided within ten days. We must devote all our efforts to it, hoping to achieve something. Discussions on the system of the party and the state do not seem difficult to resolve by abandoning past grievances. Political disputes easily lead to military conflicts, and internal strife is worse than external attacks. Betraying oneself is often done unconsciously. In the current situation, one must either be Goujian who tasted gall or Tian Heng who jumped into the sea. Both require the same goal of unity. The common people are deeply moved by Goujian's unremitting efforts to strengthen the country. Why not disregard the sword and laugh while offering one's head to atone for one's mistakes? However, this must not be what you all allow. Looking south to the Yangtze River, I urgently express my words, hoping you will consider them. Feng Yong, bowing down.

▲ Telegram to Awaken the People: To all organizations, legal entities, newspapers, and people from all walks of life, after the Northeast Incident, Feng Yong managed to survive and enter the customs to face the elders of Guanzhong, feeling deeply ashamed. However, as a military scholar, I have nothing to do with major plans and was imprisoned by enemies. Turning around in a small room, life and death were uncertain. Finally, I was put on a ship to seek exile in a distant wilderness. The turbulent waves overwhelmed me, and my body and mind were lost. By falsely relying on the elders, I was able to cross the sea after hardships and set foot on the national soil again. Meditating and thinking about the pain, I cannot remain silent. As the saying goes, "One must insult oneself before others insult one." and "One must attack oneself before others attack one." In the past twenty years, the atrocities committed by Japan and other imperialists against our people have been almost incessant. The accumulated weakness of the country is certainly a clear reason. However, if during this period, people had worked together to build the country, without military conflicts to damage the country's strength and without political disputes to lose the people's hearts, ten years of recovery and ten years of education, even if we could not conquer Wu, how could Wu conquer us? This is the first thing I cannot remain silent about. In today's world, economic competition precedes military affairs. We claim to be a country established on agriculture, but the value of food imports exceeds 200 million yuan annually. As for exporting raw materials and importing finished products, we have become a market for international exploitation and plunder. It is difficult to count those who sacrifice their flesh and blood as sacrifices. Even if Japan does not engage in military aggression, its detailed and concrete understanding of our country's economic situation, which is transformed into policy and applied as a neighbor, could it not uniquely control our fate? Those who extravagantly talk about military matters today, although they may have some insights, have they ever had precise scientific plans for national production development and distribution? How can China's agriculture gradually move towards industrialization, and how can we save the country through industry, all are still dreams. If we want to build, we will only sigh that we have the will but not the power, and we will be even more ignorant. This is the second thing I cannot remain silent about. The rise of a nation, in addition to strength, values accurate consciousness. Today, the entire country is accustomed to comfort, extravagance, and licentiousness, without end. The sounds of crying from hunger and cold are not heard, and the tragedy of overturned nests and destroyed homes is ignored. Some are warlords, some are politicians, some are corrupt officials, and some are greedy officials. They claim to overthrow, but they themselves embody these ills. Many students boast of being promising youths, but they mostly squander their parents' money and act out farces to obtain diplomas. They regard pleasure and indulgence as legitimate lifestyles, boasting of neglecting their studies as being superior and shouting insults to teachers as being great. They indulge in romance and have long become parasites of society. Whenever national humiliation occurs, they also run around and shout slogans, but they have their own intentions and separately conceived plans. It is impossible to find even five percent of pure and passionate blood, let alone working on the ground and leading the people for a long time. In recent days, military training is loudly advocated, but can the youth truly maintain this serious spirit, live in groups, and cultivate the habit of discipline? If there is doubt about this, then waking up and walking in sleep is enough to be secretly laughed at by the enemy. If consciousness is improper, then the aim will be inaccurate. This time, the Japanese people's tyranny should be seen not as attacking our weaknesses in action, but rather as attacking our weaknesses in consciousness. The ancients said that the greatest sorrow is the death of the heart, and physical death is secondary. Have the hearts of the people of the country died? This is the third thing I cannot remain silent about. In summary, these three points all stem from insulting and attacking ourselves, which is due to our own ignorance. I hope that all the elders, brothers, sisters, and aunts in the country will resolutely break through the barrier of self-deception and become the government's support and the government's supervisors. Then, a nation can be revitalized through difficulties, which can be used as an admonition. Feng Yong, with the remaining years of his life spent in worry and committed to the country, is willing to take up the whip and rush to the battlefield for the sake of the people. I hastily express my words, feeling deeply anxious. Feng Yong, bowing down.

The Depression of Japanese Commerce in Qingdao 77

▲ Our Economic Sanctions are Gradually Showing Results

Qingdao Correspondence: Since all sectors of this city have consistently implemented economic sanctions against Japan, Japanese industrial and commercial businesses in Qingdao have suddenly shown a state of depression. Some small industrial and commercial businesses have even closed down as a result. The recent business conditions of Japanese industrial and commercial businesses are investigated separately as follows: (1) Spinning Mills: Although the major spinning mills founded by Japanese people in Sifang, Cangkou, and other places are still continuing to operate, there are no sales of their products in Qingdao at all. Even those shipped to other ports are only 20 to 30 percent, and the rest are piled up in warehouses. Although there is no problem with funding for the time being, the public warehouses are full and cannot accommodate any more. Most are barely holding on. (2) Cotton yarn, cloth, sugar, paper, and miscellaneous goods are all in a state of complete shutdown. No one is making new purchases, and even agreed-upon goods cannot be delivered. Also, there are no orders for marine products, and there are even cases of returning the remaining balance of already delivered goods. (3) Exported goods: There are currently no shipments. (4) Banks and shipping companies: Their business has been greatly affected by the negative resistance. Also, because Chinese banks and pawnshops refuse to pay pawn tickets and refuse to sell silver dollars, business has become sluggish. The Japanese-Qingdao shipping company has stopped scheduled sailings due to a sharp decline in cargo and passengers. (5) Various factories: Unlike spinning mills, many of their employees have become idle, and many cannot maintain operations due to funding issues. Among them, many small industries that were recently established, such as printing, ironware, and miscellaneous goods, have temporarily closed down. (6) Small merchants who specialize in serving Chinese people have completely stopped operating. Observing from the above situation, if our country can persevere to the end and cut off all transactions, then Japanese industrial and commercial businesses will have no foothold in Qingdao. (November 4th)

The 19th Regular Meeting of the National Government 78

The National Government held its 19th regular meeting on the 6th. The attendees were Ma Fuxiang, Wang Boqun, Chen Guofu, He Yingqin, Zhang Ji, Shao Yuanchong, Ding Weifen, Yu Youren, and Dai Chuanxian. Yu Youren presided over the meeting, and the following matters were discussed: (1) Resolved to announce the revised "Regulations on the Management of Narcotic Drugs." (2) Resolved to announce the "Rules for Issuing Medals and Swords to the Army, Navy, and Air Force." (3) Resolved to approve the resignation of Huang Huilong, a military advisor to the government, and replace him with Gu Renfa. (4) Resolved to appoint Li Bingrong as a counselor to the Military Council. (5) Resolved to appoint Fan Zize as the chief of staff of the Yushan Jin Border Area Pacification Office, and Zhang Zongfen as the chief of the staff department of the office. (6) A report from the Executive Yuan stated that the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Railways had jointly submitted a report stating that the "Regulations on Punishing Violations of Police Regulations" should be applied to fulfill their duties. This matter was submitted to the 45th State Council meeting of this Yuan, which resolved to approve the ministry's proposal and forwarded it to the National Government for review and compliance. Resolved to approve the matter. (7) A report from the Executive Yuan stated that the Ministry of Interior had submitted a report approving the Hunan Provincial Government's submission of a table classifying the counties in the province, requesting that it be forwarded for review and promulgation. The ranking of counties listed in the table conforms to Article 4 of the County Organization Law and the regulations on classifying counties in various provinces. It is proposed to follow the established practice and announce it after approval by the Yuan. Resolved to approve the matter. (8) A report from the Executive Yuan stated that the Ministry of Education had submitted a report stating that Kuang Qiyong, a native of Wuxi, had founded schools and spent a total of more than 240,000 yuan over the years, and requesting a special commendation. A detailed report of the facts was attached and submitted specifically requesting the Yuan to forward it for commendation. This matter is in accordance with Article 5, Paragraph 2 of the "Regulations on Commending Donations for Establishing Schools." Resolved to commend the matter. (9) A report from the Control Yuan stated that Control Commissioner Shao Hongji had submitted a report on the investigation of the Henan flood situation, requesting that it be forwarded for review and implementation. Resolved to forward the matter to the Flood Relief Committee. (10) A report from the Control Yuan stated that Liu Xiuyue, the magistrate of Liuhe County, Jiangsu, had neglected his duties, and the facts were clear. It requested that he be handed over for disciplinary action in accordance with the law. Resolved that Liu Xiuyue be dismissed and barred from re-employment for one year.

Principal Zhong Xiu still not safe: Since the Flying Cloud steamer of the Tongyuan Yiji Steamer Bureau on the Dongshan Inner River was hijacked, several hostages have been released one after another. However, Ms. Chuan Zhongde, the principal of Zhongxiu Primary School in Dongshan, is still being held in the bandit's lair. Although she is a primary school principal, her monthly income is only more than 30 yuan, which is only enough to make ends meet. This time she was kidnapped, not only is she financially unable to find a way to rescue her, but her old mother has just died and there is no one else. Therefore, the bandits regard her as a god of wealth, but she is actually a poor female teacher without a place to stand.

Jiangyin 80

Lights out, military and police maintain order: The Huaming Electric Light Company, due to the failure of the main engine last time, was out of power for a week, which affected the market and caused losses to merchants. Last night (the 4th) around 8 pm, the cylinder broke again and the lights went out, turning the city inside and outside into a dark world. For the sake of security, the military and police immediately worked overtime to patrol to prevent accidents.

Robbery case in Zhangjiagang solved: The daughter of the late farmer Sheng Lianzhen of Zhangjiagang, Nansha Township, married into the Meng family in Shanggang, Nangang on the 28th of last month. Her dowry was quite large and was robbed. Ma Huaizhong, the police officer of the 2nd squad of the Wangjiatai garrison, learned that it was committed by Zhang Guanquan and others from Zhangjiagang. He immediately captured three people and sent them to the county on the 4th. After interrogation by Judge Wu Cheng, Zhang Liangcheng confessed that he was from Fujian and had been a militiaman in Sanjiali in previous years. On the 27th, he was instigated by Zhu Manlang and others at a teahouse in Wangjiatai and forced to go to the Sheng family. I was outside the door and got two yuan after the incident. Xu Cailang confessed that he did not know about the robbery of the Sheng family. Later, Zhu Manlang gave me two yuan. Zhang Guanquan also confessed without denial. After interrogation, they were taken into custody to await interrogation of the plaintiff.

Wuxi 81

Major fire in Tongyun Road: The back house of the Xinmeifu cooked meat shop in the Tongyun Road Market outside Guangfu Gate suddenly caught fire around 3 am yesterday (the 6th). At that time, the wind was strong, and it spread to the neighboring Daqinglou restaurant in an instant. It was extinguished after firefighters from various sections arrived at the scene to put out the fire. A total of one bay and two sections of Xinmeifu and two bays and two sections of Daqinglou were burned down, with a total loss of more than 10,000 yuan. Fortunately, they had fire insurance, so the loss was slightly less.

Yuanfeng Sauce Garden in Sanliqiao robbed: The Zheng Yuanfeng Sauce Garden in Xiaosanliqiao outside the North Gate was opened by the Chen and Fan brothers and also managed Yida Kerosene. At around 7 pm the day before (the 5th), six robbers suddenly came, each holding a pistol, and broke into the counter under the pretext of buying sorghum. They cut the telephone line and forced the accountant Yuan Shusheng to hand over the key. When Shusheng refused, he was slapped in the face by the robbers and gestured to open the safe with a pistol. Then they searched arbitrarily and robbed more than 200 yuan in paper money, two gold rings, and two gold watches, with a total loss of more than 300 yuan. After the robbers got the loot, they fled in the direction of Datian'an and Dahechi.

Changzhou 82

The High Court investigates the opium case: On May 3 of this year, the Wuyi County Court sent bailiff Liu Shiqin to Xixiasu in the third district to investigate the opium dealer's office, Wang Chengji, resulting in the bailiff Liu being beaten by the crowd. The opium dealer Wang Chengji and his wife Wang Yinshi took the opportunity to escape. The bailiff reported to the court and verified the injuries. Chen Baoxin, the police officer of the first police station of the public security second sub-bureau of the town, failed to assist the court in arresting the suspect in advance, and was suspected of dereliction of duty. The Public Security Bureau immediately ordered him to be suspended from his duties. Afterwards, Wang Shuliang, the director of the Benniu Public Security Bureau, learned that the opium dealer's wife Wang Yinshi and his partner Yun Jusheng and others had sneaked back, and immediately sent police officer Wang Zheng to lead the police to arrest them for interrogation. Many people were implicated. Wang Chengji also turned himself in. After the prosecutor completed the investigation, he prosecuted the criminal court and sentenced Wang Chengji, Wang Yinshi, Yun Jusheng, etc. to imprisonment and fines. Yesterday (the 5th), news came that the chief prosecutor of the High Court paid close attention to this case. Because the police officer Chen Baoxin of the town police station was suspected of protecting the opium dealer Wang Chengji and dereliction of duty, he was impeached according to law, ordering the Wuxian Local Court to try the case according to law. The court specifically scheduled to open the court on the 7th of this month, summoned Liu Shiqin, the bailiff of the Wuyi County Court, Li Zonggang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, Chen Baoxin, the police officer, and Xie Ling, the chief of the third district. All the summons have been sent to the Wuyi County Court, ordering the police to serve them according to law, ordering all the summoned to come to Suzhou for trial on schedule.

Canal contractor commits suicide: Chen Jiesan, the contractor for the dredging of the Wuyi Canal, had an office in Yongqing Temple in the south of the city. He suddenly committed suicide by jumping into the river late on the 5th. On the morning of the 6th, his subordinates retrieved his body from the river and found a suicide note, which roughly stated that he was saddened by the invasion of the Japanese pirates and the unrest in the country, as well as the inability to settle the wages for the canal workers, so he was angry and made this decision.

Zhenjiang 83

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association organizes ten-person groups: The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association believes that the country is in extreme danger recently, and that there is no way to survive without self-salvation. Without unity, there is no way to save oneself. Therefore, it has launched the organization of anti-Japanese national salvation ten-person groups. Ten people are a group, based on the relationship of occupation, neighborhood, friends, and relatives, vowing to resist Japan and save the country, revitalize the nation, engage in training in life and thought, and strive to carry out the anti-Japanese national salvation movement. Yesterday, it had drafted organizational rules, creeds, and oaths, asking all sectors to organize quickly.

More than 20 groups pray for peace and unity: The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Zhenjiang County Farmers' Association, the Chamber of Commerce, the Education Association, the Journalists' Association, and more than 20 other groups sent a telegram to Mr. Wang Jingwei, Mr. Hu Hanmin, Mr. Cai Yuanpei, and two other gentlemen in Shanghai yesterday, and forwarded it to all representatives, roughly stating that since the completion of the Northern Expedition by the National Revolutionary Army, the people thought that they could enter a period of prosperity. However, for several years, there have been frequent internal conflicts and external aggression, especially by the Japanese bandits. They destroyed our Jinan and now have destroyed our Northeast. The national crisis is urgent, and the country will be destroyed soon. Fortunately, all parties have abandoned their differences to seek sincere unity to jointly face the national crisis. The people are all celebrating with joy. The party can truly save the country and make the last attempt to govern the country by the party. However, in the past ten days, several preparatory meetings have been held, but political opinions have become increasingly divergent, and there is unrest in the city. The people are weeping and begging, willing to starve to death, fearing that the Republic of China will be destroyed. The association and others deeply know that the meetings held by both the Beijing and Guangdong parties this time are to save the nation from danger. They also know that you must be able to see the people's expectations today, shorten the meeting preparations, take national affairs as the premise, and take the political program and policies as the basis to establish a national salvation strategy to rescue the people from the fire and water. If there are people who dare to take risks, or pretend to cooperate, or speak arbitrarily, and even try to obstruct and destroy, the righteousness will be revealed, and the will of the people will be there. The association and others swear to lead all the people of Jiangsu Province with the determination to support peace and unity, and to work together. At the same time, we also dare to use the determination to wish the peace conference to break through all difficulties and achieve a satisfactory result. We anxiously express our words and are overwhelmed by the anticipation.

Organize a research association on Japanese issues: The Provincial Propaganda Committee convened a meeting of all capital city departments in the Provincial Party Department yesterday and decided to organize a research association on Japanese issues. Zhang Zhou, Zhou Huapeng, Jiang Xiaochen, and He Kaiyi were asked to draft a charter and submit it to the next meeting for discussion. Yesterday, an introductory statement and organizational method were drafted and sent to all sectors for information and implementation.

Qingjiang 84

Stores That Suspended Business Resume Normal Operations: The silk fabric, general merchandise, and sundry goods stores in Huaiyin have, since the 28th of last month, all suspended business under the pretext of inconvenient financial turnover. As of yesterday (the 2nd), it has been five days and they have not yet reopened. The local Anti-Japanese Association happened to be in a period of reorganization. Yesterday, Dai Boqiu, a standing committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, and the original mediators Ye Zijun and Gu Xunru, went to the county government to discuss solutions with County Magistrate He and Qian Danquan, a standing committee member of the Party Department. The result was that since the merchants said they suspended business due to financial inactivity, the Japanese goods that should have been sealed up by the merchants who suspended business could be used as collateral for the various money houses. Each merchant could justify their actions, and there would be no need for sealing even after the establishment of the new anti-Japanese association in the future. Everyone considered this method to be appropriate for a time. At 4 PM the same afternoon, the Chamber of Commerce summoned the directors of various industries for a tea party. The merchants of various industries, who only sought profit, also considered these methods to be satisfactory and agreed to resume business as usual today (the 2nd). By about 7 AM this morning, the 18 stores that had suspended business indeed reopened their doors, and the storm of strikes came to a temporary end.

Ningbo 85

A Major Incident in the Inspection of Japanese Goods: Some crew members and sailors of the Xin Jiang Tian Wheel recently harbored deep resentment because they secretly carried Japanese goods and were repeatedly discovered by anti-Japanese inspectors. Yesterday morning, the ship arrived in Yong from Shanghai, loaded with 240 packages of foreign salmon dried fish, rumored to be Eastern Ocean dried fish, purchased by 11 fish shops in Yongbu, including Hengtai and Tongfuchang. The sailors wanted to test the inspectors' eyesight and responsibilities, so they first took five or six dried fish ashore. As a result of the test, the inspectors detained them. Later, when the whole case of dried fish was taken ashore, the inspection team did not detain it for some reason. Therefore, the sailors, using the slogan that the inspection team was being influenced by treacherous merchants, gathered five or six hundred crew members and hooligans and made things difficult for inspectors Xu Zhen and Li Henian. They dragged them to the Ning Shao Wharf, beat them severely, and tied them to the pier, claiming they should be paraded through the streets. For a time, many people echoed this. The two chiefs of the police station and the supervisors of the Public Security Bureau tried to persuade them without success. The police went to mediate, but many were beaten. Order was greatly disrupted for a time. Later, after Chen County Magistrate, Mao, Chief of Public Security, and Lin, a member of the Party Committee, persuaded them in many ways, Xu and Li were finally released and taken to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation into the source of the dried fish for verification. Unexpectedly, Zhuang, a patrol officer from the Second District Office, planned to escort Xu and Li to the Public Security Bureau. When they reached the entrance of Hejia Lane, they were intercepted and severely beaten by the sailors. The two took the opportunity to escape into the China Merchants Bureau and closed the iron gate. The crowd smashed the signboard of the bureau. It was not until a company of security guards arrived that order was slightly restored. As a result, Xu and Li were escorted from the China Merchants Bureau to the Public Security Bureau, and the 240 pieces of dried fish were sealed by the Chamber of Commerce in the China Merchants Bureau's warehouse.

▲Wang Boling's Talk: Wen Guangyi, director of the Military Training Department of the Shanghai University Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation, accompanied by Gu Bu Guanghua, instructor Chen Yinzhangde of the department, visited Wang Boling, the central government's specially appointed director of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Army Training Office, at the Municipal Government yesterday. The central government is very sincere in training the Shanghai student army, and I also have great enthusiasm and hope. I believe that in the near future, the central government will issue firearms. If the central government does not issue them, you enthusiastic students will ask the central government for them, and I will also ask the central government for them." (2) When will instructors arrive? Wang answered, "Today (the 6th), the central government has sent more than 140 people to Shanghai, who can be assigned to various schools around tomorrow." Wang answered, "The central government's training outline has not yet been issued. After the General Association of Chinese Students Studying in Japan Moved to Shanghai 94

▲Compatriots Within the United Nations Vow to Resist Japan to the Death

▲Dispatch Personnel to Organize Branches to Increase Strength

▲The Issue of Transferring Schools Is Still Difficult to Resolve Temporarily

▲Please All Sectors to Assist Detained Students

(Shanghai News Agency) The General Association of Chinese Students Studying in Japan moved to Shanghai on the 29th of last month, renting the Huadong Apartment on Malong Road as its headquarters. It began working on the 4th of this month, striving for the anti-Japanese movement. Yesterday afternoon, the association held a meeting with reporters from various newspapers and news agencies on the third floor of the YMCA on the side of Jincheng Education Bank to report on the situation of the association's move to Shanghai. The Shanghai News Agency reporter recorded the following reports:

▲Reasons for Returning to China: There are four main points: (1) Excessive oppression by the Japanese police; (2) Must fulfill the duties of the representatives' congress of each school; the purpose of our 3,000 students is because the environment in Japan is harsh and unfavorable for progress; (3) To promote peaceful unification and jointly resist foreign enemies; (4) To cooperate with the revolutionary masses in the country to resist Japan together until death.

▲Reasons for Invasion: The main reasons for the violent Japanese invasion of our Eastern Provinces are: (1) Domestic economic panic leading to political panic; (2) From a semi-colonial status to a purely colonial status; (3) Intending to obtain a base for the Second World War.

▲Anti-Japanese Work: (1) Make efforts in anti-Japanese work that students in domestic universities cannot reach; (2) Promote peaceful unification to produce a strong government to resist Japan together; (3) Go to the countryside; (4) Will never return to Japan for studies before the violent Japanese troops withdraw.

▲Publish Publications: It has been decided to publish the "Exposure" tri-weekly, which has already been printed, and organize a research association, divided into five departments: political, economic, diplomatic, social, and military. The research findings of each department will be published in another magazine for the reference of the people of the country.

▲Organize Branches: Representatives have been sent to Beijing, Tianjin, Guangzhou, and other places to be responsible for organizing branches to carry out a unified anti-Japanese movement and increase strength.

▲Unwilling to Register: More than 200 returning students have registered in the branch associations, more than 120 have registered in the Municipal Education Bureau, and more than 1,700 have not registered. The total number of returnees is about 2,000 or more, accounting for four-fifths of the total number of students studying in Japan. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued instructions, ordering students who have already registered with the Municipal Education Bureau to transfer to Nanjing Central University, the local Jinan University, the engineering department of Jiaotong University, and Jiangxi Agricultural College as auditors. However, the returning students are unwilling to transfer schools. Yesterday, Qin Yuanbang, the general affairs director of the association, visited Lin Ben, the representative sent by the Ministry of Education, and stated the reasons as follows: (1) Unwilling to disperse students, reduce anti-Japanese strength, and hinder the national salvation movement; (2) If registered, they must transfer to domestic universities, and their student status in Japan will be cancelled in an invisible way; (3) After registration and receiving a considerable living allowance, they must transfer to various schools; (4) Due to the fact that their facts and level of study cannot be transferred to domestic universities as auditors.

▲Request for Assistance: Wen Yongzhi, a member of the executive committee of the association, was arrested by the French police at the association's office in Huadong Apartment at 9 PM the night before (the 5th), and documents and books were searched, and the office was sealed off. Wen Xiangping, a member of the standing committee of the association, was also arrested at No. 30, Xiafei Lane, Xiafei Road, at 1 AM on the same night. Luo Jianbing (female), the accountant of the branch association, and Lei Zhensheng (female), a member, were also arrested at No. 15, Yide Lane, Lafayette Road, at 12 AM on the same night. In addition to investigating the truth, the association sent a representative, Mou Yu, to the Xujiawan French Police Station at 2 AM yesterday (the 6th) to negotiate, but to no avail. Then they went to the local court to request notification to the French police authorities to allow them to meet the arrested students. The reply was that it was not within their scope of responsibility and it was inconvenient to forward the request. The association believes that the members are all patriotic people who returned from Japan and are actively working hard for the anti-Japanese national salvation work, and their studies have been sacrificed. However, the violent Japanese have still not withdrawn their troops and continue to invade, so the anti-Japanese work must be stepped up. The members have been arrested and urgently need assistance from all parties to request their release. It has been decided to separately request powerful assistance from the representatives of Ning and Guangdong, the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Administration, the Municipal Education Bureau, the Taxpayers' Association, the Municipal Anti-Japanese Association, and other agencies this morning. The anti-Japanese groups of various universities have already been working hard for this and ask all parties to act as a backing for negotiations, it is said.

Tense Work at the Municipal High School Association Library 98

▲Reading Room Uses Open-Shelf System

▲Borrowing Department Reduces Borrowing Fees

▲Delivery Department to Open Soon

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commercial Library has two reading rooms that collect Chinese and Western magazines, currently with more than 400 types. They are completely displayed on the shelves, and important encyclopedias and other items are also fully displayed. They trust that readers can value public morality and implement an open-shelf system to make it convenient for readers. Recently, an exhibition of books on the Sino-Japanese issue was held. Since the previous day, it has been handled according to the revised new regulations, reducing the borrowing fee. The annual fee is only one yuan, and there is no limit to the number of times various books can be borrowed within a year. Therefore, there have been many new borrowers recently. Since the preparations for the delivery department began, it has been less than half a month. Thousands of people have requested these regulations. Currently, 160 people have filled out and submitted guarantee letters. Therefore, the preparation work has been extremely busy in recent days. The date for the start of the actual book delivery is not far away.

Relief Boxing Match Closes This Morning 104

丨Over 3,000 Attendees丨

The second relief boxing match was held last night at 9:00 PM at the same venue. The evening featured a gathering of famous professionals. Westerners accounted for nineteen out of ten attendees. Director Zhang of the Nanjing National Arts Hall delegated Zhu Guofu and Weng Guoxun to attend and observe. The program consisted of eight events. The important matches were in the first half, featuring Shanghai's leader Ross against India's champion Tao Kefu, and in the second half, Clayton against Maurice, lasting until 12:45 AM.

(1) Thomas (Suffolk), 130 lbs, vs. Cooley (Shanghai), 131 lbs - Thomas wins.

(Course) The fight was scheduled for four rounds. Thomas defeated his opponent about halfway through the second round, ending the match.

(2) Shi Weili (Mailing), 135 lbs, vs. Niger (Shanghai), 138 lbs - Shi wins.

(Course) Initially, Niger attacked fiercely but did not gain an advantage due to poor defense. Later, Shi Weili rallied and gained a superior position. At the end of the sixth round, the referee declared Shi the winner.

(3) Peito, Hudson, 128 lbs, vs. Bauer (Luoshan), 132 lbs - Peito wins by two pounds - Peito wins.

(Course) A match between the US and French naval champions. One was Peito, the leader of the US fleet, and the other was Bauer, the French naval champion. The Frenchman defended tightly and struck powerfully. The American did not attack recklessly but landed many blows. In the first four rounds, both had their ups and downs. In the fifth and sixth rounds, the Frenchman attacked more than he defended. At the end of the round, the referee declared the American the winner. The audience was dissatisfied, and boos arose. In all fairness, a draw would have been the most equitable outcome.

(4) Ross (Shanghai), 170 lbs, vs. Tao Kefu (Hong Kong), 80 lbs - Ross wins.

(Course) This was the highlight of the first half. The two initially maintained a stalemate. From the fourth round onwards, Shanghai's Ross landed several powerful blows, gradually gaining the upper hand. In the fifth round, Tao was punched in the face and fell to the ground, unable to continue. The bell saved him. In the sixth round, Tao woke up and attempted to strike horizontally. In the seventh round, Ross was resilient and punched powerfully. In the eighth round, Ross maintained his advantage and secured the final victory.

(5) Bernie (Hudson), 128 lbs, vs. Bena (Manila), 138 lbs - Bernie wins.

(Course) The two were evenly matched. In the third round, Bena lost his defense and was knocked to the ground. He repeatedly called out ten times but remained motionless on the ground. Bernie won. Bernie was the first to win by knocking out his opponent.

(6) Walker (Western Police), 150 lbs, vs. Qin Ning (Mailing), 155 lbs - Qin Ning wins.

(Course) In the first two rounds, Walker had a slight advantage. The third round was a draw. In the next three rounds, Qin Ning showed strength, and the final victory went to Qin Ning.

(7) Dulin (Hudson), 158 lbs, vs. Baron (Suffolk), 153 lbs - Dulin wins.

In the sixth round, Baron's face was unprotected and he was repeatedly hit, ultimately leading to his defeat.

(8) Clayton (Western Police), 147 lbs, vs. Maurice (Suffolk), 147 lbs - Clayton wins.

The Voice of Resistance Against Japan

— Ji Ping

The brutal Japanese call our three northeastern provinces "Manchukuo," and even have so-called "South Manchuria" and "North Manchuria." This is because they have long harbored intentions of aggression and have established terms with anesthetic effects. We should rightfully call them the "Three Northeastern Provinces" or the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, and should not echo them. However, newspapers and magazines still use "South Manchuria" and "North Manchuria," as if tacitly acknowledging these nonsensical terms. How can this be?

Recently, someone suggested changing the name "Japan" to "Bandit State" to make the name fit the reality. I strongly agree with this proposal. Like Japan, which is so fierce, cruel, and unscrupulous, committing all kinds of evil, disregarding justice, and lacking humanity, its actions are nothing short of a "Bandit State." If my colleagues in the press agree that this is not wrong, please change the name "Japan" to "Bandit State" from now on.

Rotary Club Narrative

This is Education! 106

A very enlightened boss of the new era said to one of his part-time employees:

"It's time. You should go to class."

The employee, who was loyal to the store, looked at the clock and then at the boss and said, "I want to take a day off today. The classmates all say that I am too enthusiastic in class, as if I am supporting the teacher."

The boss was surprised by this unexpected answer. He didn't say anything at the time. Later, he met a friend who understood the inside story of education and talked about this matter. That friend thought for a moment and said with a smile:

"Taking fewer classes can save some money on transportation and buy more books to read, which is much better than listening to professors' lectures. Your colleague is more accurate in calculating this."

The Plundering of Treasures from My Palace by the Japanese寇 in the Year of Gengzi 107

— Zheng Yimei

The Japanese寇 have repeatedly invaded China, as recorded in history books. In the year of Gengzi, the Boxer Rebellion occurred. The Eight-Nation Alliance trampled our land. The imperial gardens were burned. The emperor fled in disgrace. It was a major upheaval in the Qing Dynasty. When the Eight-Nation Alliance marched straight in, the Japanese slaves acted as the vanguard and were in charge of the gatekeepers. My friend Zhang Lianweng, who was a resident of Beijing, knew an old palace eunuch named Jia. Jia witnessed the events of that year firsthand. He said that the Japanese slaves were more greedy and ruthless than any other country in looting the palace. They seized many treasures from the forbidden area. According to what I (Jia) know, there was a jade bottle. The bottle was twelve feet tall and purely emerald green. In the summer, when placed in a room, it would naturally generate coolness within five or six feet. It was like King Zhao of Yan's summer-cooling beads. Empress Dowager Cixi loved it very much. The Japanese slaves hurriedly plundered it. Carelessly carrying it, it fell to the ground and broke in the middle. The broken bottle was still carried to the Eastern Island by the Japanese slaves. The eunuchs picked up the small, uncollected pieces left on the ground. Later, antique dealers sold them to Western countries for more than 100,000 gold, which shows the value of the bottle. There was also a crystal horse, as large as an ordinary riding horse. The whole body was crystal clear. The palace maids often straddled it after a bath to play. The lingering fragrance of the beauties was immeasurably precious. Also, there was an ivory mat used by Emperor Yongzheng. Thin slices of ivory were shaved and woven into a dragon-patterned mat. The fineness of the workmanship was like the work of ghosts. It is said that it took half a year, day and night, to weave this mat. After it was completed, the person who made it lost his eyesight due to excessive consumption of eyesight. The power and blessing of the autocratic emperor can also be seen from this. Other coral trees were made, with gold dust used as mud, and bright moon-like beads were carved from white jade into boxes. The Japanese slaves took whatever they wanted, not knowing how much they carried away. The essence of the imperial palace was almost completely lost. It is extremely heartbreaking to talk about. This time, during the Shenyang Incident, the Northeast was rich in storage and plundered at will. What is even more regrettable is the Siku Quanshu. The value of cultural relics cannot be compared with jade and silk. Looking north, my grief is endless.

World Snippets 108

— Haike

A Ship That Won't Sink

One of the greatest inventions in the world is the kind of self-rescue ship that does not sink. This new invention has been used on lifeboats and is very effective. It involves cutting out a piece of wood like a slice of watermelon. Then, no matter what the situation in the water, it can immediately return to its original state. Recently, another amazing invention was announced to the world. It is indeed a ship that will not sink. The inventor is a Frenchman named Joseph Dharttain. He made a model of an Atlantic mail ship, twelve feet long and half a ton in weight, for shipbuilding experts to test. They used iron bars to poke many large holes in the hull below the waterline. If a large ship were poked with these holes in the same way, it would undoubtedly sink to the bottom of the sea in one or two minutes. But this model ship, even with holes all over it, only dropped one or two inches and still floated proudly on the surface of the water. If such ships were to become popular all over the world, it would truly be a blessing for sailors.

— Yiweisheng

The Shanghai Commercial Press branch window recently displayed maps of the Three Northeastern Provinces and statistical charts of China's area and population, and comparison charts of the US and China's economy and education. Catering to the current situation, it attracted the attention of many passers-by.

Recently, beggars resembling disaster victims have been seen sporadically in the evenings.

Japanese Marine Corps sentries still patrol day and night. Five people form a team.

The weather is getting colder. Every morning, many working-class people sit and bask in the sun along the western side of the road.

North of Dadelie, there are many Jiangnan peddlers selling hot water caltrops in the mornings.

The Cantonese Grand Theater is currently performing non-Cantonese plays.

There are about twenty stalls selling crabs.

Many Japanese and Chinese female students are seen on the road when going to and from school. They all wear uniforms. However, Chinese female students seem to pay great attention to the decoration of their hair, shoes and socks.

The students of Japanese schools here are simple and unadorned. I have never seen anyone wearing "high-end Western clothes" or long hair with slanted ointment. Some of the Chinese students have the demeanor of young masters. Those who see it sigh.

Every night after 8:00 PM, there are still White Russian volunteers wearing iron helmets and full armor. Every six or seven people form a small team, followed by several Chinese and Western Indian Japanese patrol officers. The White Russian volunteers march and stand in formation. The other patrol officers walk casually in scattered teams.

A Record of a Beauty Treatment Demonstration 110

— Nvpu

In my spare time after class, I was sitting alone and bored. I read a novel advertisement in the newspaper from Sincere Company. For a moment, I was moved by the attraction and curiosity, so I drove to see it.

The beauty salon is located on the second floor. Although it is not large, it is beautifully decorated and contains artistic ideas. The four walls are hung with portraits of Hollywood movie stars after using Max Factor beauty products. They are full of dazzling things and are beautiful to see. The stage is set in the center of the room. Steel chairs are arranged in front. There are many Chinese and Western women among the guests. The staff cordially greeted them and seated them in order. The demonstrator is a Western woman, who is the so-called Mrs. Xishi. She gave a speech in English about the efficacy of Max Factor beauty treatments. A gentleman from the company translated. After the speech, she asked one of the guests to try it first. The audience all held their cheeks in their hands and shrank back. Suddenly, a person next to the seat stood up and responded, "Okay." Looking at her, it was a middle-aged woman of about forty years old. The translator led her to the stage and asked her to sit down. The demonstrator observed her for a long time. (The color of each person's face is different, so the powder used is also different.) She applied cleansing cream to her face and gently wiped it off with a powder brush. Then she mixed and applied rouge evenly. Next, she gently swept the eye area with eyeliner. She drew eyebrows that resembled a crescent moon. She thinly applied lipstick on her lips. She used white powder to apply it to all parts of her arms. After it was finished, she was graceful and beautiful as peach and plum blossoms. What was previously called a middle-aged woman is now transformed into a graceful lady. The omnipotence of science is truly not a false statement. Returning home, I was moved and wrote it down.

Buting Caozhai Grand Talk Club

A Countryman Comes to Shanghai Again (9) 111

— Bao Tianxiao

"Why has the value of Zhu Mao risen like this?" He wanted to elicit the countryman's words, so he pretended to ask for advice.

"Probably because of the customs duties on going abroad," the countryman nodded and shook his head, constantly sucking on his dry cigarette holder.

"That's right, that's right!" The detective thought to himself secretly. "I once heard people say that many Communists have been abroad. Zhu Mao is also a student who has studied abroad and has been to the West. Now he says that their value has increased because of going abroad, which is even more correct. Who would have thought that such a countryman is a Communist?"

"Does going abroad increase value?" The detective asked faintly.

"How can it increase value?" The countryman again made his great remarks. "In this day and age, everything must be contaminated with foreign air. Instead of speaking Chinese, you have to speak foreign languages. Instead of wearing Chinese clothes, you have to wear Western-style clothes. Instead of wanting a Chinese wife, you have to marry a foreign woman. In fact, don't we have everything in China? Bringing a little foreign air is considered fashionable." After giving this theory of pacifying the inside and resisting the outside, his eyes were still fixed on the young man in a suit who was reading the newspaper opposite, as if he still had some lingering anger over the dispute over the erotic picture book.

"Why did the value of Zhu Mao increase because he had been abroad?" The detective pressed on. This was like a hunting dog seeing a rabbit, how could he let it go easily?

"This is easy to understand. That pig hair is used for fertilizer and cannot escape the hands of us farmers. Besides fertilizing the fields, it has no other use. So those butchers who kill pigs have to buy it from us. Now I hear that that kind of thing is also foreign. Foreigners have come up with new tricks. Besides fertilizing the fields, it has other uses. What exactly is it used for? He secretly concealed it, but once they bought it, the pig hair soared. It used to be a few dollars a load, but now it has risen to tens of dollars a load."

"What a few dollars a load? Tens of dollars a load? I'm asking you about Zhu Mao."

"That's right! I'm telling you the price of pig hair."

"I'm asking you about the Communist Party's Zhu Mao."

"I'm telling you about the pig hair for fertilizing the fields."

"Bah! It's really confusing." The detective was greatly disappointed. He wanted to take this opportunity to get a great credit and win a great reward. He didn't want the Zhu Mao in our hearts to turn into the pig hair in his heart. He was fooled by this country old man. He was so angry that he still lay down and slept, pretending to be asleep, listening to what the third-class guests had to say.

The Yarn, Cotton, and Silk Markets are Dull and Lifeless 118

The yarn market remains weak, with a very soft trend. Due to the financial emergency and ongoing national disputes, commerce cannot develop, resulting in an extremely bleak market atmosphere. Furthermore, large investors are selling off, while new purchases are relatively few. The future of the yarn market is still in a slump.

▲ Major Investors Selling Off "Rén Biāo" (Yarn Exchange Standard Contracts): At the opening of the "Rén Biāo" market, the atmosphere was quite flat, with prices falling by 7 or 8 qián. In the second and third rounds, prices rebounded. As a result, near-term contracts fell by 1, 3, or 5 qián, while far-term contracts rose by 1 or 4 qián. In the afternoon, the market situation fluctuated again, with prices falling by 1, 2, 4, or 6 qián. The total trading volume was 29,500 bales. It was found that Yuánfēng sold 4,600 bales, Yìchǎng sold 1,100 bales, and Dàchāngchéng sold 1,100 bales. Tàixīng bought 2,000 bales, Yìyú bought 1,350 bales, and Zhèndà bought 900 bales. The Cotton Market Continues to See Factory Sell-offs 119

The cotton market is very weak. Due to the loose exchange rates, the silver price for calculating the cost of imported cotton is very cheap, even 1 or 2 taels lower than the previous day. Furthermore, the Shēn Xīn textile mill has purchased over 10,000 bales of Indian and American cotton. Manufacturers are still hedging a large number of future contracts. However, merchants from the Hàn帮 (Hubei) region and some cotton merchants are holding tight and not releasing their cotton, and their intention to squeeze shorts this month has not diminished. Furthermore, Reuters reported that Russia has 1,000 train cars of cotton ready to be dumped on the European market, indicating a surplus of cotton worldwide. Therefore, large investors and manufacturers are continuously selling off, creating a very dangerous situation.

▲ The "Hàn Biāo" (Hankou Cotton Exchange Standard Contracts) Market is Affected by Imported Cotton: At the opening of the "Hàn Biāo" market, prices fell by 2 qián due to the weakness of American cotton and the sharp rise in silver prices. Later, prices rebounded due to some short covering, resulting in a flat market. In the afternoon, news of a large batch of imported cotton being traded caused the market to fall slightly by 5 fēn to 1 qián. The total daily trading volume was 120,000 dan. It was found that Héngdà sold 2,000 dan, Dàfú sold 9,600 dan, Méijì sold 2,800 dan, Tàixīng sold 5,600 dan, Yìchéng sold 3,100 dan, Chángfēng sold 3,900 dan, and Chánghé sold 2,000 dan.
