Next, Jiang Xiangqing, a representative of the colleagues' association at Shishi News, reported on the final requirements of the colleagues' association. The following were then discussed: (1) How to resolve the layoff dispute at Shishi News. It was resolved that the association would submit the settlement plan agreed upon by the management to the colleagues' association, and at the same time, the final settlement plan proposed by the colleagues' association should be submitted to the management for agreement. If it could not be resolved by Sunday, it would be submitted to a temporary meeting for discussion. (2) Scheduling a temporary meeting. It was resolved that the meeting would be held at Shuji Primary School in Tianhou Palace at 2:00 PM on the 8th of this month (Sunday), with the standing committee members acting as chairmen of the meeting. (3) Reorganizing the association into a journalists' guild. It was resolved that Tang Demin, the original proposer, would draft a proposal and submit it to the meeting for discussion. (4) Zhu Yingpeng proposed applying to the municipal government for land to be used as the guild's base. It was resolved that this would be submitted to the meeting for discussion. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau Opens Special Half-Price Section 174

Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau, located at the corner of Shilu and Sanmalu, has been known in the city for its excellent selection of goods and low prices. However, the bureau is not satisfied with this. In order to stand out in the silk and satin industry, it has established a half-price section within the bureau, selling various new silk, Ge, Ling, and satin products at reduced prices to reward customers. Among them, printed soft satin, Huaxiang Ling, Jindi crepe, Tianxin crepe, and plain wool Ge are the most affordable and high-quality. It is also said that the bureau's self-made winter women's coats and capes are uniquely styled and have a modern feel, and are especially welcomed by well-known ladies, daughters of wealthy families, and social stars.

Launch of the Benevolent King National Protection Dharma Assembly 175

In Buddhism, there is the Benevolent King National Protection Sutra and the Benevolent King National Protection Dharma. Its responses can alleviate national disasters and repel foreign invaders, with many clear effects in ancient and modern times, both domestically and abroad. At present, domestic and foreign troubles are pressing each other. People in the Buddhist community cannot bear to sit idly by, so they have launched a Benevolent King National Protection Dharma Assembly, inviting the highly virtuous Dharma Master Chi Song to read the sutra and preach the Dharma at the Gongdelin Monastery to pray for peace. The initiators are Zhu Ziqiao, Wang Yiting, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, and other prominent figures in Sichuan. Tonight, by the Carlton edge, Buddhist and patriotic men and women will surely be busy and come to listen to the high monks preach the Dharma.

New Domestically Produced Suit Cufflinks and Buttons 176

It is reported that Mr. Ding Fu has invested to establish the Great China Factory, with the "Champion" brand trademark, specializing in the production of suit cufflink buttons, in order to resist enemy goods and recover lost rights. The factory address is selected at Tianshou Lane, Qingyun Road, Zhabei, and manufacturing has already begun. The products are of excellent quality and the prices are low to meet the needs of all sectors. It is hoped that all patriots will be happy to adopt them.

Dr. Sun Zhiying Found Not Guilty in Lawsuit 177

Dr. Sun Zhiying and her sister Zhongying have been operating the Cide Hospital in Wufu Lane in this city for over twenty years. Someone sued her for neglecting her duties in the First Special District Court. After several court summonses, the court ruled that the evidence presented was insufficient and dismissed the case, finding the defendant not guilty.

Yuanhexie Ginseng, Bird's Nest, and Seafood Store Opens 178

Yuanhexie Northern Goods and Seafood Store on Wuzhou Road, Hongkou, has completed its new building and will officially open tomorrow (the 8th). In order to promote business, the store has established a ginseng, bird's nest, and white fungus section. It is said that the prices of all goods are particularly low to attract customers.

Newly Released Domestically Produced Stencil Ink 179

Since the outbreak of resistance against Japan, Gongsheng Printing Ink Factory on Jiaotong Road, which specializes in the production of printing ink, has strived to produce stencil ink. Due to the precision of the machinery and the suitability of the quality, those who have tried it all say that it is sticky but not greasy, and it can be considered a top-quality stencil ink. The factory is rushing to produce tens of thousands of pounds, packaging it in cans for sale, and setting the trademark as "Star Brand". The colors are divided into blue, black, and three types, and in order to resist Japanese goods, the price is particularly low.

Invention of Linglong Soy Sauce 180

Wang Xinji has recently invented "Linglong Soy Sauce" with the Magpie brand, which has recently arrived in Shanghai for sale. It is completely different from various soy sauce essences on the market and is even better than imported soy sauce. Its characteristic is that the umami taste is particularly strong, and the less used, the more savory it is. This kind of "Linglong Soy Sauce" must be exposed to sunlight for four or five years to form this essence. It is now distributed by the general manager of Huashang Sanhe Company at 56 Nanjing Road. The price is one yuan per bottle, but it is now sold at a special price of only eight jiao. Sincere, Wing On, and food stores all act as agents. For days, those who have purchased in bulk have been extremely enthusiastic.

Establishment of the 16th District Branch of the City Federation 181

The 16th District Branch of the Citizens' Federation held its inaugural meeting yesterday. Zhu Maoqing, Wang Zhaocheng, and Chen Jicheng were elected as the presidium and conducted the formalities. The chairman gave an opening speech and reported on the preparation process. The election began, and Wang Maoqing, Chen Jianqiu, Wang Zhaocheng, Zhao Kecheng, Zhu Yunsheng, Wu Jichang, Chen Zhixin, Huang Xianqing, Yang Sihui, Lu Fengzhu, and Xu Kaijun were elected as executive committee members. Ye Haojun, Chen Jicheng, and Zhang Baokang were elected as alternate members.

Shenxin No. 2 Factory Negligence Case Verdict: Not Guilty 182

According to Shenshi News, there was a negligence incident in the cotton cleaning room of Shenxin No. 2 Cotton Mill on Yichang Road on the 22nd of last month. The workers all rushed to escape, resulting in six female workers being trampled to death. The police alleged that the emergency exit set up by the cotton mill was not opened in accordance with the regulations and that there was suspicion of negligence. Therefore, the First Special District Court was prosecuted for negligence of duty resulting in death and injury. The Special Court approved the filing and placed Zhu Xianfang, the manager of the cotton mill, and Zhang Yiming, the supervisor, under detention and bail for questioning. Yesterday morning, the Second Criminal Court of the Special Court conducted an interrogation. First, Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, presented the details of the investigation of the case. Zhu and Zhang, the two defendants, retained lawyers Wang Fushang and Wu Linkun for defense. They argued that at the time of the fire in the cotton mill, the emergency exit was directly in the path of the fire, and there were concerns that sparks would fly into the cotton room and spread the fire, so it was temporarily closed. Moreover, the female workers did not die in the fire, but were trampled on by other workers rushing to escape, causing the disaster. Therefore, it can be known that the death of the deceased was unrelated to the closure of the emergency exit, and there was no negligence. Various female workers also testified to this effect. Judge Feng Shide impartially investigated the situation and concluded that the case was debated. The court declared not guilty on the spot and released the defendants.

News from Various Trade Associations 183

▲Silk and Brocade Printing Industry: The Silk and Brocade Printing Industry Association held its inaugural meeting at the New World Restaurant on Nanjing Road at 6:00 PM on the 5th. Representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, including He Yuanming, representatives from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, including Hu Yuqi, representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, including Sun Mingqi, legal advisor Wang Zhengshao, and over twenty member businesses such as Zhu Zijing, Wang Menglu, and Li Shisheng, attended the meeting as scheduled. Representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Municipal Chamber of Commerce delivered guiding speeches. The constitution was passed on the spot, and executive committee members were elected. The election results showed that Chuan Gongwei, Li Yebai, Qin Yingzhai, Shen Liucun, Tong Gang, Zhang Jinglu, and Cheng Shao'an were elected as executive committee members, and Zhu Wenyan as an alternate member. The meeting concluded with a banquet, ending in joyful spirits.

▲Liangshao Industry: The Liangshao Liquor Industry Association convened its members yesterday afternoon for a general membership meeting. Over thirty members attended, including Huang Yuming, He Xiangsheng, Zhang Guanshou, Ni Yangzhou, Shi Youqing, Zhang Zheming, and Du Baochu. Huang Yuming chaired the meeting, which proceeded as scheduled. The chairman reported on the association's efforts to organize the National Salvation Volunteer Army and the participation of various industry employees in the Volunteer Army Municipal Defense Corps. Then, discussions began, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the issuance of membership certificates to all members, it was resolved and passed. (2) Regarding the request from the Tobacco and Alcohol Monopoly Bureau to relay registration information to all members, it was resolved that the association would survey its members to gather and submit the information. (3) Regarding the price increase of the local yellow wine monopoly fee, it was resolved to notify all members to continue paying the monopoly fee according to the existing rates of 16 cents and 32 cents. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

▲Restaurant Industry: The Restaurant Industry Association convened its 19th regular meeting at 3:00 PM on the 4th. Cheng Kefan chaired the meeting, and the following matters were discussed: (1) A letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's office for collecting and paying business tax on behalf of businesses, stating that the extended deadline for submitting business tax forms had passed and requesting personnel to urge submission, was discussed. It was resolved to notify all members and non-members again to promptly submit the forms and comply accordingly. (2) A letter from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association regarding the establishment and implementation of inspections by the association's inspection team was discussed. It was resolved that the matter had been handed over to the inspection team to conduct separate inspections, and any remaining Japanese goods would be sealed and stored, pending further instructions. (3) A letter from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association regarding the labeling of enemy goods samples to avoid confusion was discussed. It was resolved to notify the members. (4) The association's general affairs section requested a two-week leave, to be temporarily handled by Shao Zaihang and Zhang Shaoping. (5) A proposal to support the unified peace conference, eliminate internal private views, and implement a united front against external aggression was discussed. It was resolved and passed. Other minor matters were also discussed. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

▲Cosmetics Industry: The Japanese Goods Inspection Committee and the Executive Committee of the Cosmetics Industry Association held a joint meeting yesterday afternoon. Ma Jisheng was publicly elected as chairman. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. After the chairman's report, the standing committee proposed whether to re-inspect vendors in the industry. It was resolved that manufacturers should affix "inspected" seals, while vendors should affix "sealed" seals. It was requested that inspection committee members in each district continue thorough inspections to avoid omissions. Subsequently, the executive committee meeting discussed matters, including Liu Shixiong's proposal on how to handle goods wrongly confiscated by various anti-Japanese associations. Fu Keming reported that Sanyou Industrial's "Xing Xing Shuang" (a cosmetic product) had been wrongly confiscated by the Anti-Japanese Association in Xiashi. The association had sent a letter to certify that it was entirely a domestic product. It was resolved that, following the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's reply, the matter should be handled according to the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association's Announcement No. 12. It was resolved to inquire with each manufacturer whether they had reclaimed the original goods. Afterward, the following resolutions were passed: (1) That Paris Company be admitted as a member of the association according to the association's constitution. (2) That the membership application of Tongyixiang, introduced by Committee Member Liu Shixiong, be referred to the investigation department for review and processing. (3) That the business tax declaration form should be certified by the association. It was resolved to refer it to the investigation department for review and certification. (4) Regarding the Shanghai Trade Associations' Tariff Research Committee's receipt of a letter from the Finance Bureau stating that manufacturers who sell goods outside of their manufacturing premises are still required to pay taxes as vendors, it was resolved to convene all trade associations to handle the matter jointly. The meeting adjourned, the bell having already rung six times.

Weather Report 184

The Xujiahui Observatory issued a weather forecast at 4:03 PM yesterday, stating that the weather in the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas is occasionally cold. There are extremely strong seasonal winds from the northwest to the northeast in Shandong, the Yellow Sea, the East China Sea, and the Taiwan Strait. A storm is located northeast of Mindanao and will continue to move northwest. A cyclone in the Sea of Japan is intensifying due to the passage of a low-pressure system and is moving toward the east-northeast. The center of the storm was located within 120 miles of the intersection of 13 degrees north latitude and 127 degrees east longitude at approximately 6:00 AM this morning. Also, within the 24 hours preceding 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 61.7 degrees and the lowest was 42.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 56.3 degrees and the lowest was 45.5 degrees.

Reader Correspondence

A Message from Korean Compatriots 185

(20,000 Return Home, Losses Exceed 20 Million Yuan)

Since the occurrence of the tragic incident, many compatriots residing in Korea have been returning home expeditiously. Recently, with the outbreak of the Northeast Incident, out of concern for safety, no fewer than 20,000 compatriots have been returning to China one after another. In their departure, they have all abandoned their assets and returned alone. Years of hard work have been swept away. Only a few remain, but their assets have been depleted, leaving them in a position where they want to leave but cannot, and want to stay but cannot. The reason is that, over the years, they have extended considerable credit. In these times, Koreans are stubbornly refusing to pay, believing that war is imminent and that compatriots will inevitably leave sooner or later. Real estate cannot be sold, only abandoned. Movable property can be sold, but after clearing debts, there is no remaining money left to sustain life. Business is sluggish due to the distress of the Koreans, and the situation is unspeakable. Consuls in various places do not observe the actual situation of the overseas Chinese, only offering protection, but what use is protection in reality? In short, the total loss of assets of the overseas Chinese should be over 20 million yuan. Among the overseas Chinese merchants, those from Jiaodong in Shandong are the most numerous. It is unknown what methods compatriots have to save them.

Letters to the Editor 187

Dear Editor,

Today, I read in your esteemed newspaper that the 15th meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association decided to exempt Korean ginseng from the boycott, and the resolution was approved with a plan to be drafted by the Secretariat. After reading this, I was greatly astonished. If such unnecessary items can be exempted from the boycott, then the word "boycott" can be ignored, and there is nothing left to boycott. I have been doing business in Korea and Japan for a long time and am very familiar with the production and sales of Korean ginseng. I dare to present the following to the nation: Korean ginseng is produced in Kaesong, Korea. Since the annexation of Korea by Japan, the Governor-General's Office has established a special ginseng monopoly bureau. The ginseng sold to China is entirely manufactured by the monopoly bureau, which collects a monopoly tax of over one million taels annually. It is then exclusively sold by Mitsui & Co., a Japanese conglomerate. Shanghai is the largest market. After Mitsui & Co. ships it to China, it is further distributed by the four major firms on Xian Gua Street: Fuchang, Dechang, Baoda, and Yuanchang. The price of Korean ginseng is extremely low in Korea. The Governor-General's Office buys it from the locals for only 18 yuan per catty. After passing through several hands, the retail price is over 100 taels per catty. Approximately 50,000 catties are sold to China annually, resulting in an annual loss of about 5-6 million taels for our country. Even in normal times, the government should increase taxes or even ban imports of such trivial items, considering the significant financial loss. Moreover, in the present circumstances, there is even less reason to allow imports. The officials of the Anti-Japanese Association believe that they should sympathize with the Korean petition. However, they may not know that the Korean Chamber of Commerce is entirely a Japanese commercial organization, with only a few Koreans as mere decorations. If they consider that the owner of Korean ginseng is the Governor-General's Office monopoly bureau, and the seller is Mitsui & Co., with no connection to Koreans at all, then there is no reason for them to petition. I sincerely hope that the directors and supervisors of the Anti-Japanese Association will not be exploited by the enemy. This is my earnest prayer. Zhang Baonian, 686 Furen Lane, South Chengdu Road, November 4th.

To the Editor,

In your newspaper's shipping news column on the 6th of this month, there was a news item about the resignation of the head of the shipping department, stating that Zeng and Li took turns holding the position and that Li resigned voluntarily. These details are completely untrue. Mr. Zeng Guangqing had already been transferred to the position of head of the business department, and Mr. Li Yuncheng was solely responsible for the shipping department. There was no resignation. This is based on inaccurate information. I hope your newspaper will promptly make a correction. Addressed to: Shen Bao Newspaper Office, General Administration of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company under the National Government, November 6th.

To the Editor,

I read yesterday's local news column in your esteemed newspaper, "Yu Qiaqing Discusses Shipping Bonds," which stated that Yu Qiaqing told people that the funds would be used to establish a shipping bank with five million yuan and allocate five million yuan to various Chinese shipping companies. These are not facts. The Ministry of Finance is discussing and approving the issuance of these public bonds, and this is true. However, the sections stating that the plan was agreed upon by Yu Qiaqing and Minister Song, and the details of the allocation, are not true. I am writing this letter to inform you and hope that you will make a correction. Addressed to: Shen Bao Local News Editorial Department, Shanghai Shipping Association, November 6, 2011.

Yesterday, I read in your newspaper that party members in Jiangsu Province were promoting the peaceful settlement of the Jiangxi telegrams, and my humble name was listed, which greatly surprised me. I have not been consulted or informed about this matter beforehand. Peaceful unification and joint resistance against foreign aggression are what the people of the country hope for. I especially hope that all parties will abandon their prejudices and not create rifts that would expose weaknesses and be ridiculed by foreign countries. The wording of this telegram places blame on Comrade Hu Hanmin, which could cause division within our party. This is not what I wish to say. It is clear that someone has fabricated the list and included my name. I am writing this special letter to correct this. With respectful greetings, Shen Bai, a party member from Changshu County.

Social News

Marshal Foch's Diary of the European War Translated by Gu Angruo 189

The enemy forces between the Aisne and Meuse rivers were greatly shaken and soon began to retreat. On November 2nd, Bussancy and Doulcon were successively captured. On the 3rd, the northern part of the Argonne was completely cleared, and the heights of Belval were also occupied. The army on the left bank of the Meuse River advanced to Thennes. On the 4th, French and American forces crossed Stonne and Le Chesne, invaded the forest south of Bairon, advanced along the Meuse River, and approached Stonne.

I warmly congratulated Commander Pershing and asked him to continue his attack towards the Meuse River, advancing upstream from Barzun while exerting maximum effort to extend to the right bank.

A separate armistice agreement has been concluded between France and Austria, and Austrian troops have withdrawn from French territory. I had requested Commander Pershing to deploy the American Second Army for assistance several days ago. (To be continued)
